1. The TV signal in the room is not very good. It is not a high-definition signal. name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior Queen Room
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted July 31, 2023
msg:The front desk of the hotel was very nice and helped us upgrade 2 rooms to the executive floor on the 17th floor. There is a very large communal lounge area on this floor. Very big sofa. The breakfast in the hotel is also good, and the coffee is surprisingly delicious. When checking in, remember to register the license plate number with the front desk for easy access. A package with a ferry ticket is recommended. The cruise ship goes at night.
DAY1
9:30 Depart from Shanghai by car
11:30 The car enters the parking lot of Hotel Nikko Wuxi, address: No. 9 Yongle East Road
11:45 Walk to Xishengyuan (Yongle Road store) for lunch, about 450 meters away, address: No. 112 Yongle Road, next door to Xinsifang Food
Check in at the hotel at 12:25 (remember to register the license plate number with the hotel when you check in, so that you can enter and exit)
12:40 Arrive at the hotel room
1. The canal view king bed room booked on Ctrip is 856 yuan/night, including 2 breakfasts + 1 ancient canal boat ticket for two people (it is recommended to go after dinner in the evening, the pier is at the starting point of Nanchang Street opposite the hotel. Sit first at night There are few people in the class, starting at 18:00, every half hour)
2. Opposite the hotel is Nanchang Street, you can move around freely after check-in. The battery car on Nanchang Street is 15 yuan per person, and 20 yuan per person for a round trip. If you can walk, it is recommended to sit in the past and walk back. There are not many people with the tea color, so you can buy a cup and taste it.
3. Behind the hotel is Nanchan Temple, free tickets, please ask for 20 yuan per person. The food street around Nanchan Temple is average, so it is not recommended to buy. There is an antique market that you can browse around.
4. For dinner, you can go to Laoniuwoli (Nanxiatang store) near the hotel. We will divide into two routes. I will ride a bicycle to get a seat at 16:30, and I will call a special car for the elderly hotel to go to the place for dinner. The hotel is about 900 meters away from the hotel. Address: Building 7, Nanxiatang Cultural and Creative Park, N1955, Nanxiatang Street. It opens at 16:30 in the evening. It is best to go as soon as it opens, and you need to wait for a seat if it is late. His quantity is large and the price is affordable. The four of us have six dishes, a bowl of noodles and a bottle of beer for 281 yuan.
5. After dinner, the four of them borrowed bicycles and went to Nanchang Street to take a boat. The boat ride takes about 50 minutes. There will be a few stops in between.
6. The morning buffet breakfast starts at 6 o'clock, and there are few people at 6:30. 7:30 began to crowd up.
DAY2
8:45 Check out the car and drive out of the hotel to Lingshan Giant Buddha
9:45 Arrive at Lingshan Giant Buddha, Address: No. 1 Lingshan Road, Binhu District, Wuxi City
11:30 Drive out of Lingshan Giant Buddha
12:30 Arrive at Suzhou Jinji Lake Lakeside Xintiandi underground parking lot
12:45 Arrive at Xinmeihua, Suzhou Center for lunch, address: No. 410, Building 68, Area H, Suzhou Central Plaza, Xinggang Street (4th Floor, Xingyuehui, Suzhou Center, Suxiu Road)
13:45 Depart Suzhou
15:30 Arrive at home in Shanghai
1. Tickets for Lingshan Giant Buddha are free for seniors over 70 years old with their ID cards, and 50% off for those over 60 years old.
2. Tickets for 1 big and 1 small on Dianping online are 270 yuan. 2 large and 1 small 480 yuan.
3. There is a battery car in the scenic area at 40 yuan/person, which can go back and forth.
4. The parking fee of Lingshan Giant Buddha Scenic Area is 15 yuan for free parking, and the 2-hour parking fee of Jinji Lake Lakeside Xintiandi underground parking lot is 5 yuan.
5. The toll from Shanghai to Wuxi is 50 yuan, and from Wuxi Lingshan Giant Buddha to Suzhou is 60 yuan. Suzhou to Shanghai 25 yuan.

msg:Ok. Come to recall the terrible experience of "Escape from the Dead" at the Nikko Hotel. My son and I took a taxi to the Nikko Hotel at two o'clock in the afternoon on the 14th. We booked for three nights and checked out on the 17th. Get ready to play near South Chang Street. The room we first gave us was 1628. After we came in, we found that we couldn't see the wide canal in the picture of Ctrip, so we changed to 1518 at the front desk. I didn't feel much when I first came in. Later, I ordered a takeout and took a break after eating. At that time, I vaguely felt a strange smell. My son said it was the smell of sweat from the clothes, so I believed it. After sleeping all afternoon, I still had the peculiar smell, because my son was sure that I didn't doubt the smell of sweat. I went out at around 6 o‚Äôclock and came back at 8 o‚Äôclock. I took a rest. I took a bath myself, soaked the clothes, and after washing, I urged my son to take a bath and soaked his clothes. When I left the bathroom to blow dry my hair, I smelled something wrong. The room was filled with a strong nasal smell, similar to the pungent smell of rural toilets and chicken coops. My head also felt a bit painful. I yelled my son. No, we can't stay and change rooms quickly! I put on a mask in the room and called the front desk. The front desk said that they would come up to see us and change the room. I asked them to wait for a while while my son was taking a shower. After waiting for half an hour for my son to take a shower, I packed up my things, rearranged my luggage, and rearranged all the clothes and towels I dried. I called the front desk and called for someone to come up immediately. It was past 10 o'clock by this time. A guy at the front desk came, and his son met him at the gate. As soon as he walked in, he said that the smell was too great and he must not be able to live. So I helped lift our luggage, and we got 1628. Opening the luggage and taking out the supplies is equivalent to moving in again. That was exhausted. Later, I knocked on the door twice to deliver fruit and a female manager came to apologize. I said it was too late, let's take a break and talk about it tomorrow. I had a headache and a dry throat, so I ate a bit of the fruit I brought. Drowsy and go to bed more than 11 o'clock.

The next day, the duty manager Eric called and explained to us that it was the smell of the sewer at first, and then that it was a leak of freon from a burnt out refrigerator. He checked Baidu and said I could check it too, and said it was a little okay. I said it was so pungent. Will it be harmful to the body? I asked them to issue a written explanation of what kind of gas it is and the harm to the human body. Then Eric called again and said that they could not issue this written statement. The engineer can come up and explain to us what this gas is and does not harm the human body. I said yes, let the workers come up. After waiting for some time, Eric knocked on the door and said that he should apologize to us, saying that it was not the smell of Freon but the ammonia leak. The change of attitude seemed to be very sincere, and said that they would deliver fruit, and breakfast was okay. We did not continue. Talk too much. In the past two days, we didn‚Äôt even bother to walk around, just order takeaways or occasionally go out for dinner in the evening. But doubts always exist in my heart, what kind of gas is this? Why one would say that Freon and the other would say that ammonia leaks, how harmful is it to the human body? From beginning to end, I kept asking what kind of gas it was and they didn't give me a written answer. On the morning of the 17th, I woke up early and checked Zhihu. The shocking ammonia water in it would cause death and made me shudder. Constant ammonia can cause people to be poisoned. I think of my headache that night and my wise decision to insist on changing rooms. If we don‚Äôt change rooms, no one knows that we stay in the air-conditioned enclosed space that smells like that, and it‚Äôs night again. Sleeping until dawn, I don‚Äôt know what terrible consequences it will cause! I trembled all over, feeling scared! I took my son to travel and stayed in countless hotels since I was young. For the first time in my life, I encountered such a serious accident with a refrigerator. I never thought that the danger would be in the hotel room! A burst of anger came to my heart, and the hotel must explain it! I called Eric and the hotel must waive our three-day room fee, and let us have a physical examination after returning home to compensate for our mental losses. We reserve the right to recourse. They came to the room twice to negotiate the matter. Sadly, the Nikko Hotel did not face up to their mistakes. I renewed my stay the next day because of the flight delay and took off in the morning. I went to check out at five o'clock in the morning on the 18th. They did not agree to waive my three-day room charge and put the higher-level female manager who came to my room the day before. I called out and said that only one of the exemption of room fees and physical examination in Wuxi (Wuxi only) can be selected. And there is no room for flexibility. I'm here to travel. My child is here to participate in the closed summer camp. Our time is well arranged. We can't go and check as they ask. We just want to go home and wait for my son to go home. To do a check. In the end, they deducted my room fee for four days, and one day was unavoidable. There was no promise, which means you love to sue you to sue! As a service industry, occasionally one or two bugs are not cleaned in place, which can be understood and forgiven, but it is a matter of life and death and cannot be easily forgiven! Because this time is my next time I may be you and your favorite person! And he or she may not be as lucky as me every time!
